  * grade_story_107.txt (grade=6.5)
    The premise and combination of elements are highly original, avoiding common tropes. However, some phrasing ("folded me like a bad envelope," "lean as driftwood") touches on the familiar. While the overall style is distinctive, moments like the stranger's exposition feel slightly functional rather than entirely organic. The emotional nuance is present but could be deepened beyond the protagonist's stated weariness and memory of applause.

  * grade_story_106.txt (grade=6.5)
    The core concept is original (farmer/bathysphere/magic heirlooms). However, the prose occasionally dips into ornateness ("lazy halos," "whispered promises," "dripping lineage," "beckoning constellations," "untarnished horizon") bordering on purple prose. The phrase "objectively biased" is awkward and feels unnatural. While not entirely formulaic, these elements weaken its claim to flawless originality.

  * grade_story_108.txt (grade=6.0)
    The combination of elements (fantasy, music, sci-fi gadget) offers originality. However, the prose, while rich, occasionally uses slightly overwrought or repetitive phrasing ("coy malevolence" stated twice). It avoids obvious AI tells but lacks the absolute freshness and nuance expected at the highest level.

  * grade_story_105.txt (grade=5.5)
    The prose is ambitious and avoids obvious AI tells but frequently borders on purple prose ("luminous than moonlight," "woven engines humming with forbidden physics"), sacrificing clarity for richness. The combination of elements is original, but the execution feels slightly self-conscious and overly ornate in places.

  * grade_story_109.txt (grade=6.0)

The polished language sometimes lacks a truly distinctive, gritty voice. The abrupt transitions and convenient solutions hint at contrivance over organic storytelling.

  * grade_story_102.txt (grade=7.0)

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=7.9)
